\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00335}00335     \textcolor{comment}{// We wish to evaluate the strain-\/rate tensor at a value of theta}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00336}00336     \textcolor{comment}{// such that k*theta = pi/4 radians. That way we pick up equal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00337}00337     \textcolor{comment}{// contributions from the real and imaginary parts of the velocities.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00338}00338     \textcolor{comment}{// sin(pi/4) = cos(pi/4) = 1/sqrt(2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00339}00339     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} cosktheta = 1.0 / sqrt(2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00340}00340     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} sinktheta = cosktheta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00341}00341 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00342}00342     \textcolor{comment}{// Assemble velocities and their derivatives w.r.t. r, z and theta}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00343}00343     \textcolor{comment}{// from real and imaginary parts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00344}00344     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} ur = UC * cosktheta + US * sinktheta;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00346}00346 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00347}00347     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} durdr = dUCdr * cosktheta + dUSdr * sinktheta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00348}00348     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} durdz = dUCdz * cosktheta + dUSdz * sinktheta;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00353}00353     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} duzdtheta = k * WS * cosktheta -\/ k * WC * sinktheta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00354}00354 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00355}00355     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} duthetadr = dVCdr * cosktheta + dVSdr * sinktheta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00356}00356     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} duthetadz = dVCdz * cosktheta + dVSdz * sinktheta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00357}00357     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} duthetadtheta = k * VS * cosktheta -\/ k * VC * sinktheta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00358}00358 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00359}00359     \textcolor{comment}{// Assign strain rates without negative powers of the radius}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00360}00360     \textcolor{comment}{// and zero those with:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00361}00361     strainrate(0, 0) = durdr;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00362}00362     strainrate(0, 1) = 0.5 * (durdz + duzdr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00363}00363     strainrate(1, 0) = strainrate(0, 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00364}00364     strainrate(0, 2) = 0.5 * duthetadr;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00365}00365     strainrate(2, 0) = strainrate(0, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00366}00366     strainrate(1, 1) = duzdz;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00367}00367     strainrate(1, 2) = 0.5 * duthetadz;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00368}00368     strainrate(2, 1) = strainrate(1, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00369}00369     strainrate(2, 2) = 0.0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00370}00370 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00371}00371     \textcolor{comment}{// Overwrite the strain rates with negative powers of the radius}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00372}00372     \textcolor{comment}{// unless we're at the origin}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00373}00373     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (std::abs(interpolated\_r) > 1.0e-\/16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00374}00374     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00375}00375       \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} inverse\_radius = 1.0 / interpolated\_r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00376}00376       strainrate(0, 2) =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00377}00377         0.5 * (duthetadr + inverse\_radius * (durdtheta -\/ utheta));}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00378}00378       strainrate(2, 0) = strainrate(0, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00379}00379       strainrate(2, 2) = inverse\_radius * (ur + duthetadtheta);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00380}00380       strainrate(1, 2) = 0.5 * (duthetadz + inverse\_radius * duzdtheta);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00381}00381       strainrate(2, 1) = strainrate(1, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00382}00382     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00383}00383 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00384}00384   \} \textcolor{comment}{// End of strain\_rate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00385}00385 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{linearised__axisym__navier__stokes__elements_8cc_source_l00386}00386 }
